Perfect for the aspiring actor, director, artist, writer, musician or anyone else coming into LA for work or play. Nice space, very clean, tub in bathroom, about 700 sq. feet. Smart TV, wifi close to Hollywood, Silverlake, Los Feliz, Echo Park, Korea town and Larchmont. You can see Griffith observatory from the courtyard. LARGE PRIVATE BEDROOM with writing desk which looks out the window. The bed is QUEEN SIZE with a super comfortable memory foam mattress. The pillows are memory foam as well. linens are new too. There are empty dresser drawers for foldables. There is also a closet with a hamper, hangers, an iron, and ironing board. It's large enough for luggage as well. MEDIA The internet is high bandwidth with Wifi. Free sling tv (cable), hbo go, ESPN watch, and easily access your Netflix, hulu, Amazon prime accounts. The unit has an AC and fan which helps provide fresh air and white noise for a restful sleep. In the BATHROOM you will find soaps, shampoos &amp; conditioners, extra-large towels, and hairdryer. The KITCHEN is very spacious with a dishwasher, fridge, toaster, microwave, stove, oven, dishes and utensils, cookware, paper towels, napkins, several kinds of teas, coffee maker, and smoothie maker.                       <div data-reactid="1395">
                       Close to everything on the east side. In between Hollywood Blvd and Santa Monica Blvd. Near western. Minutes from silver lake, West Hollywood, and Los Feliz. Some of the best taco trucks in LA park right around the corner, so you can enjoy the way most Angelenos eat mexican food. The apartment is on the edge of Thai Town above Korea Town, so plenty of great Thai and Korean food close by. Many awesome restaurants and very hip bars are all within a mile away. Central Hollywood with it's walk of fame, amazing restaurants and bars, Arclight theater, Amoeba Records, and attractions are all 1.5 miles away.

I could not recommend this place any more for someone that just needs a nice quiet place in this area of LA.</p><span data-reactid="1555">Sshmtb</span><span data-reactid="1556">2017-02-13T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                       <li data-reactid="1557"><p data-reactid="1558">Popi got an A+ for communication. The apartment was extremely clean, decorated in a modern tone and had all of the comforts of home. The bedding was top notch and super comfy. Any questions or concerns we had, Popi was quick to answer them. It is a great unit and a great deal. Other issues: There wasn't enough toilet paper or paper towels for our trip, when I brought this to their attention, they said they will let the cleaning supervisor know this was an issue. The neighbor is a chain smoker, so her smoke can sometimes linger into the windows, she also leaves cigarette butts and ashes all over the stairs. The building manager should address this concern with her. We had several issues with the tvs being logged into other accounts, so we couldn't even watch it on more than one occasion. I was in constant communication with Popi, but this was a big bummer. I doubt it'll be an issue going forward, maybe they just weren't aware of the issue. Whoever parks at space #14 (the space on the right), is horrible at parking and there were times when I had to hop over to the passenger seat to get out of my car. The biggest bummer was having them double book the unit, then calling me the night before our trip asking me to move to another unit. I was in the middle of tucking my children in, my mom was in the hospital and getting hit with this was a little overwhelming. When I told them I was disappointed, they resolved the issue immediately and the plan wasn't changed. I understand things happen, but it caught me off guard. Overall, I would definitely recommend this place. It's in East Hollywood, away from the tourist life, but just a hop and a skip back to it. They were great hosts. Spotless unit, excellent 24/7 communication, easy access to everything. Thank you for your hospitality. </p><span data-reactid="1559">Maribel</span><span data-reactid="1560">2017-03-12T00:00:00Z</span></li>
